  59: const CREATE_TABLE_SQL = `
  60:   CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS transcripts (
  61:     client              TEXT    NOT NULL,
  62:     project             TEXT    NOT NULL,
  63:     session_id          TEXT    NOT NULL,
  64:     raw_sha256          TEXT    NOT NULL,
  65:     title               TEXT    NOT NULL,
  66:     started_at          TEXT    NOT NULL,
  67:     imported_at         TEXT    NOT NULL,
  68:     cwd                 TEXT    NOT NULL,
  69:     branch              TEXT    NOT NULL,
  70:     raw_source_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
  71:     raw_upload_permission TEXT  NOT NULL,
  72:     global_raw_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
  73:     global_clean_path   TEXT    NOT NULL,
  74:     global_manifest_path TEXT   NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  75:     repo_raw_path       TEXT    NOT NULL,
  76:     repo_clean_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
  77:     repo_manifest_path  TEXT    NOT NULL,
  78:     message_count       INTEGER NOT NULL,
  79:     tool_event_count    INTEGER NOT NULL,
  80:     cleaning_mode       TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  81:     repo_mirror_enabled TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  82:     content             TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  83:     commit_layer        TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  84:     PRIMARY KEY (client, project, session_id, raw_sha256)
  85:   )
  86: `
  87: 
  88: const UPSERT_SQL = `
  89:   INSERT INTO transcripts (
  90:     ${ALL_COLUMNS.join(', ')}
  91:   ) VALUES (${ALL_COLUMNS.map(() => '?').join(', ')})
  92:   ON CONFLICT(${PK_COLUMNS.join(', ')}) DO UPDATE SET
  93:     ${DATA_COLUMNS.map((c) => `${c} = excluded.${c}`).join(',\n    ')}
  94: `
  95: 
  96: const CREATE_FTS_SQL = `
  97:   CREATE VIRTUAL TABLE IF NOT EXISTS transcripts_fts USING fts4(
  98:     content='transcripts',
  99:     title, cwd, branch, content, commit_layer
 100:   )
 101: `
 102: 
 103: const REBUILD_FTS_SQL = `
 104:   INSERT INTO transcripts_fts(transcripts_fts) VALUES('rebuild')
 105: `
 106: 
 107: const SEARCH_SQL = `
 108:   SELECT t.client, t.project, t.session_id, t.title, t.cwd, t.branch, t.started_at
 109:   FROM transcripts_fts
 110:   JOIN transcripts t ON transcripts_fts.docid = t.rowid
 111:   WHERE transcripts_fts MATCH ?
 112:   ORDER BY t.started_at DESC
 113:   LIMIT ?
 114: `
 115: 
 116: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 117: // Types
 118: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 119: 
 120: export interface SearchResult {
 121:   client: string
 122:   project: string
 123:   session_id: string
 124:   title: string
 125:   cwd: string
 126:   branch: string
 127:   started_at: string
 128: }
 129: 
 130: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 131: // Helpers
 132: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 133: 
 134: /**
 135:  * Sanitize a user-supplied query string for safe use in an FTS4 MATCH clause.
 136:  * Strips all non-letter/digit/space characters (including single quotes which
 137:  * cause FTS4 MATCH parse errors).
 138:  */
 139: export function sanitizeFtsQuery(raw: string): string {
 140:   return raw
 141:     .replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}\s]/gu, ' ')
 142:     .trim()
 143:     .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
 144: }
 145: 
 146: /**
 147:  * Open (or create) a writable SQLite database.
 148:  * Runs schema migration on every open.
 149:  */
 150: function openDb(dbPath: string): InstanceType<typeof Database> {
 151:   mkdirSync(dirname(dbPath), { recursive: true })
 152:   const db = new Database(dbPath)
 153:   db.pragma('journal_mode = WAL')
 154:   db.pragma('busy_timeout = 5000')
 155:   return db
 156: }
 157: 
 158: /**
 159:  * Additive column migration йИ•?adds content and commit_layer if missing.
 160:  * Ignores "duplicate column name" errors (idempotent).
 161:  */
 162: function migrateSchema(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
 163:   for (const col of ['global_manifest_path', 'cleaning_mode', 'repo_mirror_enabled', 'content', 'commit_layer']) {
 164:     try {
 165:       db.exec(`ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN ${col} TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''`)
 166:     } catch (e: unknown) {
 167:       if (!(e instanceof Error) || !e.message.includes('duplicate column name')) throw e
 168:     }
 169:   }
 170: }
 171: 
 172: /**
 173:  * Drop and recreate FTS table if it doesn't have the new columns.
 174:  * Must be called after migrateSchema so the source table is up to date.
 175:  */
 176: function migrateFts(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
 177:   const row = db.prepare(
 178:     "SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='transcripts_fts'"
 179:   ).get() as { sql: string } | undefined
 180: 
 181:   if (!row || !row.sql.includes('commit_layer')) {
 182:     db.exec('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS transcripts_fts')
 183:     db.exec(CREATE_FTS_SQL)
 184:     db.exec(REBUILD_FTS_SQL)
 185:   }
 186: }
 187: 
 188: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 189: // Public API
 190: // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
 191: 
 192: /**
 193:  * Initialise schema (transcripts table + FTS virtual table).
 194:  * Safe to call multiple times йИ•?uses IF NOT EXISTS + additive migration.
 195:  */
 196: export function initSchema(dbPath: string): void {
 197:   const db = openDb(dbPath)
 198:   try {
 199:     db.transaction(() => {
 200:       db.exec(CREATE_TABLE_SQL)
 201:       migrateSchema(db)
 202:       db.exec(CREATE_FTS_SQL)
 203:       migrateFts(db)
 204:     })()
 205:   } finally {
 206:     db.close()
 207:   }
 208: }
 209: 
 210: /**
 211:  * Rebuild the FTS index from the transcripts table.
 212:  * Call once after a batch of upserts, or after any DELETE/VACUUM.
 213:  */
 214: export function rebuildFtsIndex(dbPath: string): void {
 215:   const db = openDb(dbPath)
 216:   try {
 217:     db.exec(CREATE_FTS_SQL)
 218:     db.exec(REBUILD_FTS_SQL)
 219:   } finally {
 220:     db.close()
 221:   }
 222: }
 223: 
 224: /**
 225:  * Full-text search over the transcript index using FTS4.
 226:  * Opens readonly йИ•?never writes. Returns [] when db missing or query empty.
 227:  */
 228: export function searchTranscripts(
 229:   dbPath: string,
 230:   query: string,
 231:   limit = 20,
 232: ): SearchResult[] {
 233:   const sanitized = sanitizeFtsQuery(query)
 234:   if (!sanitized) return []
 235:   if (!existsSync(dbPath)) return []
 236: 
 237:   const db = new Database(dbPath, { readonly: true })
 238:   try {
 239:     return db.prepare(SEARCH_SQL).all(sanitized, limit) as SearchResult[]
 240:   } catch {
 241:     return []
 242:   } finally {
 243:     db.close()
 244:   }
 245: }
 246: 
 247: const FTS_COLUMNS = new Set(['title', 'cwd', 'branch', 'content', 'commit_layer'])
 248: 
 249: /**
 250:  * Search restricted to specific FTS columns using FTS4 column filter syntax.
 251:  * e.g. columns=['commit_layer'] йИЂ?MATCH 'commit_layer:term'
 252:  * Column names are validated against the known FTS column set.
 253:  */
 254: export function searchTranscriptsByColumns(
 255:   dbPath: string,
 256:   query: string,
 257:   columns: string[],
 258:   limit = 20,
 259: ): SearchResult[] {
 260:   const sanitized = sanitizeFtsQuery(query)
 261:   if (!sanitized) return []
 262:   const validColumns = columns.filter((c) => FTS_COLUMNS.has(c))
 263:   if (validColumns.length === 0) return []
 264:   if (!existsSync(dbPath)) return []
 265: 
 266:   const columnQuery = validColumns.map((col) => `${col}:${sanitized}`).join(' OR ')
 267:   const db = new Database(dbPath, { readonly: true })
 268:   try {
 269:     return db.prepare(SEARCH_SQL).all(columnQuery, limit) as SearchResult[]
 270:   } catch {
 271:     return []
 272:   } finally {
 273:     db.close()
 274:   }
 275: }
 276: 
 277: /**
 278:  * Insert or update a single transcript manifest row.
 279:  * Creates schema if needed. Rebuilds FTS after write.
 280:  */
 281: export function upsertSearchIndex(
 282:   dbPath: string,
 283:   manifest: ManifestEntry,
 284: ): void {
 285:   const db = openDb(dbPath)
 286:   try {
 287:     db.transaction(() => {
 288:       db.exec(CREATE_TABLE_SQL)
 289:       migrateSchema(db)
 290:       db.exec(CREATE_FTS_SQL)
 291:       migrateFts(db)
 292:     })()
 293: 
 294:     const record: Record<string, unknown> = { ...manifest }
 295:     const params: (string | number)[] = ALL_COLUMNS.map((col) => {
 296:       const value = record[col]
 297:       if (value === undefined || value === null) return ''
 298:       return typeof value === 'number' ? value : String(value)
 299:     })
 300: 
 301:     db.prepare(UPSERT_SQL).run(params)
 302:     db.exec(REBUILD_FTS_SQL)
 303:   } finally {
 304:     db.close()
 305:   }
 306: }

+  if (typeof value === 'string') {

+  addColumnIfMissing(db, 'content', "content TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''")
+  addColumnIfMissing(db, 'commit_layer', "commit_layer TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''")
+

+    db.exec("ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN repo_mirror_enabled INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0")
+    return
+  }

/**
 * Open (or create) a writable SQLite database.
 * Runs schema migration on every open.
 */
function openDb(dbPath: string): InstanceType<typeof Database> {
  mkdirSync(dirname(dbPath), { recursive: true })
  const db = new Database(dbPath)
  db.pragma('journal_mode = WAL')
  db.pragma('busy_timeout = 5000')
  return db
}

/**
 * Additive column migration йИ•?adds content and commit_layer if missing.
 * Ignores "duplicate column name" errors (idempotent).
 */
function migrateSchema(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
  for (const col of ['global_manifest_path', 'cleaning_mode', 'repo_mirror_enabled', 'content', 'commit_layer']) {
    try {
      db.exec(`ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN ${col} TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''`)
    } catch (e: unknown) {
      if (!(e instanceof Error) || !e.message.includes('duplicate column name')) throw e
    }
  }
}

 * Drop and recreate FTS table if it doesn't have the new columns.
 * Must be called after migrateSchema so the source table is up to date.

Output:
/**
 * Transcript search index йИ•?SQLite upsert for the global transcript catalog.
 *
 * Uses better-sqlite3 (native binding) for synchronous SQLite access.
 * FTS4 full-text search on title, cwd, branch, content, commit_layer columns.
 *
 * Design notes:
 * - Schema init uses ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN for additive migrations (no version table).
 * - FTS table is dropped+recreated when column list changes.
 * - busy_timeout = 5000ms guards against concurrent writer collisions.
 * - Single-quotes are stripped from FTS queries to prevent MATCH parse errors.
 * - searchTranscripts opens readonly and never writes.
 */

import Database from 'better-sqlite3'
import { mkdirSync, existsSync } from 'node:fs'
import { dirname } from 'node:path'
import type { ManifestEntry } from '@openmnemo/types'

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Column definitions
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

const PK_COLUMNS = [
  'client',
  'project',
  'session_id',
  'raw_sha256',
] as const

const DATA_COLUMNS = [
  'title',
  'started_at',
  'imported_at',
  'cwd',
  'branch',
  'raw_source_path',
  'raw_upload_permission',
  'global_raw_path',
  'global_clean_path',
  'global_manifest_path',
  'repo_raw_path',
  'repo_clean_path',
  'repo_manifest_path',
  'message_count',
  'tool_event_count',
  'cleaning_mode',
  'repo_mirror_enabled',
  'content',
  'commit_layer',
] as const

const ALL_COLUMNS = [...PK_COLUMNS, ...DATA_COLUMNS] as const

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// SQL statements
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

function createTableSql(tableName = 'transcripts', ifNotExists = true): string {
  return `
  CREATE TABLE ${ifNotExists ? 'IF NOT EXISTS ' : ''}${tableName} (
    client              TEXT    NOT NULL,
    project             TEXT    NOT NULL,
    session_id          TEXT    NOT NULL,
    raw_sha256          TEXT    NOT NULL,
    title               TEXT    NOT NULL,
    started_at          TEXT    NOT NULL,
    imported_at         TEXT    NOT NULL,
    cwd                 TEXT    NOT NULL,
    branch              TEXT    NOT NULL,
    raw_source_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
    raw_upload_permission TEXT  NOT NULL,
    global_raw_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
    global_clean_path   TEXT    NOT NULL,
    global_manifest_path TEXT   NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    repo_raw_path       TEXT    NOT NULL,
    repo_clean_path     TEXT    NOT NULL,
    repo_manifest_path  TEXT    NOT NULL,
    message_count       INTEGER NOT NULL,
    tool_event_count    INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cleaning_mode       TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    repo_mirror_enabled INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    content             TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    commit_layer        TEXT    NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    PRIMARY KEY (client, project, session_id, raw_sha256)
  )
`
}

const UPSERT_SQL = `
  INSERT INTO transcripts (
    ${ALL_COLUMNS.join(', ')}
  ) VALUES (${ALL_COLUMNS.map(() => '?').join(', ')})
  ON CONFLICT(${PK_COLUMNS.join(', ')}) DO UPDATE SET
    ${DATA_COLUMNS.map((c) => `${c} = excluded.${c}`).join(',\n    ')}
`

const CREATE_FTS_SQL = `
  CREATE VIRTUAL TABLE IF NOT EXISTS transcripts_fts USING fts4(
    content='transcripts',
    title, cwd, branch, content, commit_layer
  )
`

const REBUILD_FTS_SQL = `
  INSERT INTO transcripts_fts(transcripts_fts) VALUES('rebuild')
`

const SEARCH_SQL = `
  SELECT t.client, t.project, t.session_id, t.title, t.cwd, t.branch, t.started_at
  FROM transcripts_fts
  JOIN transcripts t ON transcripts_fts.docid = t.rowid
  WHERE transcripts_fts MATCH ?
  ORDER BY t.started_at DESC
  LIMIT ?
`

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Types
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export interface SearchResult {
  client: string
  project: string
  session_id: string
  title: string
  cwd: string
  branch: string
  started_at: string
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Helpers
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

/**
 * Sanitize a user-supplied query string for safe use in an FTS4 MATCH clause.
 * Strips all non-letter/digit/space characters (including single quotes which
 * cause FTS4 MATCH parse errors).
 */
export function sanitizeFtsQuery(raw: string): string {
  return raw
    .replace(/[^\p{L}\p{N}\s]/gu, ' ')
    .trim()
    .replace(/\s+/g, ' ')
}

/**
 * Open (or create) a writable SQLite database.
 * Runs schema migration on every open.
 */
function openDb(dbPath: string): InstanceType<typeof Database> {
  mkdirSync(dirname(dbPath), { recursive: true })
  const db = new Database(dbPath)
  db.pragma('journal_mode = WAL')
  db.pragma('busy_timeout = 5000')
  return db
}

/**
 * Additive column migration йИ•?adds content and commit_layer if missing.
 * Ignores "duplicate column name" errors (idempotent).
 */
function tableInfo(
  db: InstanceType<typeof Database>,
  tableName = 'transcripts',
): Array<{ name: string, type: string }> {
  return db.prepare(`PRAGMA table_info(${tableName})`).all() as Array<{ name: string, type: string }>
}

function columnType(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>, columnName: string): string | null {
  const column = tableInfo(db).find((entry) => entry.name === columnName)
  return column ? column.type.toUpperCase() : null
}

function addColumnIfMissing(
  db: InstanceType<typeof Database>,
  columnName: string,
  columnSql: string,
): void {
  if (columnType(db, columnName) !== null) return
  db.exec(`ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN ${columnSql}`)
}

function sqliteBoolean(value: unknown): 0 | 1 {
  if (typeof value === 'boolean') return value ? 1 : 0
  if (typeof value === 'number') return value === 0 ? 0 : 1
  if (typeof value === 'string') {
    const normalized = value.trim().toLowerCase()
    return ['1', 'true', 'yes', 'on'].includes(normalized) ? 1 : 0
  }
  return 0
}

function rebuildTranscriptsForBooleanRepoMirror(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
  db.exec('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS transcripts_fts')
  db.exec('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS transcripts__new')
  db.exec(createTableSql('transcripts__new', false))
  db.exec(`
    INSERT INTO transcripts__new (${ALL_COLUMNS.join(', ')})
    SELECT
      client,
      project,
      session_id,
      raw_sha256,
      title,
      started_at,
      imported_at,
      cwd,
      branch,
      raw_source_path,
      raw_upload_permission,
      global_raw_path,
      global_clean_path,
      global_manifest_path,
      repo_raw_path,
      repo_clean_path,
      repo_manifest_path,
      message_count,
      tool_event_count,
      cleaning_mode,
      CASE
        WHEN lower(trim(CAST(repo_mirror_enabled AS TEXT))) IN ('1', 'true', 'yes', 'on') THEN 1
        ELSE 0
      END,
      content,
      commit_layer
    FROM transcripts
  `)
  db.exec('DROP TABLE transcripts')
  db.exec('ALTER TABLE transcripts__new RENAME TO transcripts')
}

function migrateSchema(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
  addColumnIfMissing(db, 'global_manifest_path', "global_manifest_path TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''")
  addColumnIfMissing(db, 'cleaning_mode', "cleaning_mode TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''")
  addColumnIfMissing(db, 'content', "content TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''")
  addColumnIfMissing(db, 'commit_layer', "commit_layer TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT ''")

  const repoMirrorType = columnType(db, 'repo_mirror_enabled')
  if (repoMirrorType === null) {
    db.exec("ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN repo_mirror_enabled INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0")
    return
  }
  if (repoMirrorType !== 'INTEGER') {
    rebuildTranscriptsForBooleanRepoMirror(db)
  }
}

/**
 * Drop and recreate FTS table if it doesn't have the new columns.
 * Must be called after migrateSchema so the source table is up to date.
 */
function migrateFts(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
  const row = db.prepare(
    "SELECT sql FROM sqlite_master WHERE type='table' AND name='transcripts_fts'"
  ).get() as { sql: string } | undefined

  if (!row || !row.sql.includes('commit_layer')) {
    db.exec('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS transcripts_fts')

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Public API
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

/**
 * Initialise schema (transcripts table + FTS virtual table).
 * Safe to call multiple times йИ•?uses IF NOT EXISTS + additive migration.
 */
export function initSchema(dbPath: string): void {
  const db = openDb(dbPath)
  try {
    db.transaction(() => {
      db.exec(createTableSql())
      migrateSchema(db)
      db.exec(CREATE_FTS_SQL)
      migrateFts(db)
    })()
  } finally {
    db.close()
  }
}

/**
 * Rebuild the FTS index from the transcripts table.
 * Call once after a batch of upserts, or after any DELETE/VACUUM.
 */
export function rebuildFtsIndex(dbPath: string): void {
  const db = openDb(dbPath)
  try {
    db.exec(CREATE_FTS_SQL)
    db.exec(REBUILD_FTS_SQL)
  } finally {
    db.close()
  }
}

/**
 * Full-text search over the transcript index using FTS4.
 * Opens readonly йИ•?never writes. Returns [] when db missing or query empty.
 */
export function searchTranscripts(
  dbPath: string,
  query: string,
  limit = 20,
): SearchResult[] {
  const sanitized = sanitizeFtsQuery(query)
  if (!sanitized) return []
  if (!existsSync(dbPath)) return []

  const db = new Database(dbPath, { readonly: true })
  try {
    return db.prepare(SEARCH_SQL).all(sanitized, limit) as SearchResult[]
  } catch {
    return []
  } finally {
    db.close()
  }
}

const FTS_COLUMNS = new Set(['title', 'cwd', 'branch', 'content', 'commit_layer'])

/**
 * Search restricted to specific FTS columns using FTS4 column filter syntax.
 * e.g. columns=['commit_layer'] йИЂ?MATCH 'commit_layer:term'
 * Column names are validated against the known FTS column set.
 */
export function searchTranscriptsByColumns(
  dbPath: string,
  query: string,
  columns: string[],
  limit = 20,
): SearchResult[] {
  const sanitized = sanitizeFtsQuery(query)
  if (!sanitized) return []
  const validColumns = columns.filter((c) => FTS_COLUMNS.has(c))
  if (validColumns.length === 0) return []
  if (!existsSync(dbPath)) return []

  const columnQuery = validColumns.map((col) => `${col}:${sanitized}`).join(' OR ')
  const db = new Database(dbPath, { readonly: true })
  try {
    return db.prepare(SEARCH_SQL).all(columnQuery, limit) as SearchResult[]
  } catch {
    return []
  } finally {
    db.close()
  }
}

  dbPath: string,

+): Array<{ name: string, type: string }> {
+  return db.prepare(`PRAGMA table_info(${tableName})`).all() as Array<{ name: string, type: string }>
+}
+
+function columnType(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>, columnName: string): string | null {
+  const column = tableInfo(db).find((entry) => entry.name === columnName)
+  return column ? column.type.toUpperCase() : null
+}
+
+function addColumnIfMissing(
+  db: InstanceType<typeof Database>,
+  columnName: string,
+  columnSql: string,
+): void {
+  if (columnType(db, columnName) !== null) return
+  db.exec(`ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN ${columnSql}`)
+}
+
+function sqliteBoolean(value: unknown): 0 | 1 {
+  if (typeof value === 'boolean') return value ? 1 : 0
+  if (typeof value === 'number') return value === 0 ? 0 : 1
+  if (typeof value === 'string') {
+    const normalized = value.trim().toLowerCase()
+    return ['1', 'true', 'yes', 'on'].includes(normalized) ? 1 : 0
+  }
+  return 0
+}
+
+function rebuildTranscriptsForBooleanRepoMirror(db: InstanceType<typeof Database>): void {
+  db.exec('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS transcripts_fts')
+  db.exec('DROP TABLE IF EXISTS transcripts__new')
+  db.exec(createTableSql('transcripts__new', false))
+  db.exec(`
+    INSERT INTO transcripts__new (${ALL_COLUMNS.join(', ')})
+    SELECT
+      client,
+      project,
+      session_id,
+      raw_sha256,
+      title,
+      started_at,
+      imported_at,
+      cwd,
+      branch,
+      raw_source_path,
+      raw_upload_permission,
+      global_raw_path,
+      global_clean_path,
+      global_manifest_path,
+      repo_raw_path,
+      repo_clean_path,
+      repo_manifest_path,
+      message_count,
+      tool_event_count,
+      cleaning_mode,
+      CASE
+        WHEN lower(trim(CAST(repo_mirror_enabled AS TEXT))) IN ('1', 'true', 'yes', 'on') THEN 1
+        ELSE 0
+      END,
+      content,
+      commit_layer
+    FROM transcripts
+  `)
+  db.exec('DROP TABLE transcripts')
+  db.exec('ALTER TABLE transcripts__new RENAME TO transcripts')
+}
+

+

+  if (repoMirrorType === null) {
+    db.exec("ALTER TABLE transcripts ADD COLUMN repo_mirror_enabled INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0")
+    return
+  }
+  if (repoMirrorType !== 'INTEGER') {
+    rebuildTranscriptsForBooleanRepoMirror(db)
   }
